<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:покуситься.html>покуси́ться</a> (27773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">куси́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покуситься.html>покуси́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokusítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покушаться.html>покуша́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attempt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покуситься.html>покуси́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самоубийство.html>самоуби́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokusítʹsja</b> na samoubíjstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attempt suicide</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to encroach <i>(on, upon)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покуситься.html>покуси́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужу́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:территория.html>террито́рию</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokusítʹsja</b> na čužúju territóriju (na čʹí-libo prava)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to encroach on smb's territory (on smb's rights)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покуситься.html>покуси́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokusítʹsja</b> na čʹjú-libo žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attempt [make an attempt on] smb's life</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to attempt on someone's life
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покуситься.html>покуси́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:президент.html>президе́нта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokusítʹsja</b> na prezidénta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attempt on the president's life</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покушение.html>покуше́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokušénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">куси́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покушаться.html>покуша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pokušátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покуситься.html>покуси́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attempt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покушаться.html>покуша́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самоубийство.html>самоуби́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokušátʹsja</b> na samoubíjstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attempt suicide</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to encroach <i>(on, upon)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покушаться.html>покуша́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужу́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:территория.html>террито́рию</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokušátʹsja</b> na čužúju territóriju (na čʹí-libo prava)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to encroach on smb's territory (on smb's rights)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покушаться.html>покуша́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokušátʹsja</b> na čʹjú-libo žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attempt [make an attempt on] smb's life</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to attempt on someone's life
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:покушаться.html>покуша́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:президент.html>президе́нта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pokušátʹsja</b> na prezidénta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attempt on the president's life</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a> (242)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">полъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pol</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>полы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>поло́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>floor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pádatʹ ná pol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall to the floor</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***полагаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полагаться.html>полага́ться</a> (2525)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полагать.html>полага́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полагаться.html>полага́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polagátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:положиться.html>положи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rely on, to pin one's hopes on, to bank on</li>
<li>to be due to</li>
<li>to be proper, to be in order, to be expected
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полагаться.html>полага́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>polagájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">properly, as it should be, as expected</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полагаться.html>полага́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>polagájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">is not supposed to</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полагать.html>полага́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ла<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <a href = vnd.unilang:доверяться.html>доверя́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:надеяться.html>наде́яться</a>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:полагаться.html>полага́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> + <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. п.</i>; <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:положиться.html>положи́ться</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <a href = vnd.unilang:причитаться.html>причита́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжным</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лаг-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поладить.html>пола́дить</a> (19400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поладить.html>пола́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poláditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to come to an understanding <i>(with)</i>, to get on <i>(with)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полгода.html>полго́да</a> (3080)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пол-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pol-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">góda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полгода.html>полго́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polgóda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полгода.html>полуго́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полгода.html>полуго́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полгода.html>полугодо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>half-year <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">period of half a year</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:северный.html>се́верном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полюс.html>по́люсе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полярный.html>поля́рная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полярный.html>поля́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:длиться.html>для́тся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:примерно.html>приме́рно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полгода.html>полго́да</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na Sévernom póljuse poljárnaja nočʹ i poljárnyj denʹ dljátsja primérno po <b>polgóda</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">At the North Pole polar night and polar day lasts for about <b>half a year</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***полдень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдень</a> (3482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пол-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pol-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">denʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póldenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>полу́дня</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>noon, midday
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдень</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>póldenʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at midday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пополудни.html>пополу́дни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popolúdni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the afternoon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>по́лдня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>póldnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">of midday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полдень.html>полдня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poldnjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">half a day</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> middle age</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> south</li></ol>

***поле.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ле</a> (854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*poľe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pleh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ле</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póle</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>по́ля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>поля́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>поле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>field, ground</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> margins</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> brim of the hat</li></ol>

***полевой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полево́й</a> (3061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ле</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póle</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> field
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полевы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>polevýje</b> rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>field</b> work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полево́й</a></b> севооборо́т</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>polevój</b> sevooborót</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>field</b> rotation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полевы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>polevýje</b> cvetý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wild flowers</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>field</b> flowers</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мышь.html>мы́шь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>polevája</b> mýšʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">vole</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>field</b> mouse</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полево́й</a></b> шпат</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>polevój</b> špat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">feldspar</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>field</b> spar</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:артиллерия.html>артилле́рия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>polevája</b> artillérija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>field</b> artillery</span></div></dd>

***полезный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полезный.html>поле́зный</a> (2202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льза</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólʹza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form of this adjective is the regular outcome of the Proto-Slavic stem <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*polьdzьn-</i>; the first yer was strong due to the presence of another yer in the following syllable. The actual genitive plural <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polʹz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льза</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólʹza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is phonologically unexpected, and was formed by analogy.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полезный.html>поле́зный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poléznyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)поле́знее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)поле́зней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>useful, helpful, good <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having a practical or beneficial use</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>wholesome</li>
<li>usable</li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полезть.html>поле́зть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poléztʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лазить.html>ла́зить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to climb (up, on to), to scramble</li>
<li>to get (into); to thrust the hand (into)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:полезть.html>поле́зть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poléztʹ</b> v vódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to get into</b> the water</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to thrust oneself (upon); to intrude (upon)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:полемический.html>полеми́ческий</a> (27079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">polém(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полемический.html>полеми́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">polemíčeskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>polemical</li>
<li>fervent, passionate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лени́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or directly from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лениться.html>лени́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lenítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
